 aise main vrath rakhane se pehle agar aap ye saat aasaan tips apanaate hai to aapako vrath rakhane main kabhi kisi bhi prakaar kii pareshaani nahin jhelni padegi

 Ganesh Chaturthi 2017: jaaniye kab he ganpati visarjan kaa shubh muhoort or kya he iskaa mahatvasaty tak pahunchane kaa maarg he shraadh
 
 
 1
 samay-samay par chote-chote miles lete rahe
 If you take small meals at an interval of a few hours at the time of fasting, it will keep your body's blood glucose level stable and you will not feel tired
 2
 You have to take special care of the amount of water in your body
 vrath main zyada se zyada pani pinaa chahie
 Also, coconut water, lemonade, green tea and buttermilk can also be consumed to meet the lack of water in the body
 3
 To maintain energy in the body during the fast, you also have to take care of carbohydrates
 iske liye aap aalu, tamaato, ghia, sitafal or sabudana bhi kha sakate hai
 4
 vrath main kamajori se nijaat paane ke liye kuttu kaa seven karnaa sabase behatar vikalp mana jaataa he
 Kuttu contains 70-75 percent carbs and 20-25 percent protein
 5
 Apart from this, Samak rice can also be eaten during the fast
 ye chaaval digeshan ke lihaaj se acha mana jaataa he kyonki ise pachaane main zyada mehnat nahin kerani padati he or ye jald hi diguest ho jaataa he
 6
 snacks ke taur par aapako vrath ke samay namakeen ke packets par zyada nirbhar nahin rahanaa chahie
 Instead, if you take fasting chips, fruit chaat or cucumber raita as a meal, then it will prove more beneficial for you
 7
 You can also drink fruit shakes at the time of fasting
 isse aapako energy, protein, carbo jaisi kai chijen aasaani se mil jaaengi
 8
 vrath ke dauraan hame tali hui chizon (backed chips, roasted pints) se bhi parhez rakhana chahie
 Instead, we can eat roasted makhana and dry fruits
 tippaniyan 9
 agar aapkaa vrath ke vakt meetha khaane kaa kuch zyada hi man kar rahaa ho to aise main aap gud or shahad kaa seven kar apni meetha khaane kii khwaahish ko puraa kar sakate hai
 10
 iske alaava aapako vrath main phul kriim doodh bhi nahin pinaa chahie
 Instead you should drink tone milk as it has less fat than full cream
